Trang Ngoc Dinh
solve_2 = function(a,b,c){
if(a==0){
if(b==0 & c==0){
print("Phuong trinh vo so nghiem")
}
if(b==0 & c != 0 ){
print("Phuong trinh vo nghiem")
}
else {
print("Phuong trinh co nghiem :")
print(-c/b)
}
}
else{
delta = b^2-4*a*c
if(delta <0){
print("Phuong trinh vo nghiem")
}
else if(delta == 0){
x = -b/(2*a)
print("Phuong trinh co nghiem kep x = ")
print(x)
}
else if(delta > 0 ){
x1 = (-b + sqrt(delta))/(2*a)
x2 = (-b - sqrt(delta))/(2*a)
print("Phuong trinh co 2 nghiem phan biet:")
print(x1)
print(x2)
}
}
}
solve_2(1,2,3)

Trang Ngoc Dinh
for (k in list(1,4,5,6,7,8)) {
n = k
i = 1
s = 0

while (i < n) {
if (n %% i == 0) {
s = s + i
}
i = i + 1
}
if (s == n) {
print(paste(n,"la so hoan thien"))
} else{
print(paste(n,"Khong la so hoan thien"))
}
k=k+1
}

Private Sub Button2_Click(ByVal sender As System.Object, ByVal e As System.EventArgs) Handles BtDN_17.Click

Dim connect As New SqlConnection("Server=DESKTOP-101QR58; database=QuanLyKho; Integrated Security=true")
Dim con As New SqlCommand("select * from dangNhap where tenDN=@tenDN and matKhau=@matKhau", connect)
con.Parameters.Add("@tenDN", SqlDbType.VarChar).Value = Tb1_17.Text
con.Parameters.Add("@matKhau", SqlDbType.VarChar).Value = Tb2_17.Text

Dim ada As New SqlDataAdapter(con)
Dim doctable As New DataTable()
ada.Fill(doctable)

If doctable.Rows.Count <= 0 Then
MessageBox.Show("Tên đăng nhập và mật khẩu không Hợp Lệ!", "Error", MessageBoxButtons.OKCancel, MessageBoxIcon.Error)
Else
Form2_17.Show()

End If
End Sub

Public Class Form6_Nhap
Private FileNhap As String = Application.StartupPath & "\textfile_Nhap.txt"
Private Sub Form3_Load(ByVal sender As System.Object, ByVal e As System.EventArgs) Handles MyBase.Load
Lv_17.Items.Clear()
Lv_17.Columns.Add("Mã VT", 50, HorizontalAlignment.Center)
Lv_17.Columns.Add("Tên Vật Tư", 100, HorizontalAlignment.Center)
Lv_17.Columns.Add("Đơn Vị", 80, HorizontalAlignment.Center)
Lv_17.Columns.Add("Số Lượng", 80, HorizontalAlignment.Center)
Lv_17.Columns.Add("Đơn Giá", 80, HorizontalAlignment.Center)
Lv_17.Columns.Add("Thành Tiền", 80, HorizontalAlignment.Center)
Lv_17.View = View.Details
End Sub
Private Sub Button1_Click(ByVal sender As System.Object, ByVal e As System.EventArgs) Handles BtThem_17.Click
If Lv_17.Items.Count = 0 Then
Dim ptu As ListViewItem
ptu = Lv_17.Items.Add(TbMVT_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbTVT_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(Cbb_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbSL_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbDG_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbSL_17.Text * TbDG_17.Text)
ptu = Nothing
Else
With Lv_17
Dim addit As ListViewItem
addit = .FindItemWithText(TbMVT_17.Text, True, 0, False)
If Not addit Is Nothing Then
MessageBox.Show("Mã vật tư " & TbMVT_17.Text & " Đã xuất hiện", "sss", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo, MessageBoxIcon.Error)
Else
Dim ptu As ListViewItem
ptu = Lv_17.Items.Add(TbMVT_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbTVT_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(Cbb_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbSL_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbDG_17.Text)
ptu.SubItems.Add(TbSL_17.Text * TbDG_17.Text)
ptu = Nothing
End If
End With
End If
TbMVT_17.Text = ""
TbTVT_17.Text = ""
Cbb_17.Text = ""
TbSL_17.Text = ""
TbDG_17.Text = ""
End Sub

Private Sub BtThoat_17_Click(ByVal sender As System.Object, ByVal e As System.EventArgs) Handles BtThoat_17.Click
Dim iexit As DialogResult
iexit = MessageBox.Show("Bạn có muốn thoát?", "Thoát", MessageBoxButtons.YesNo, MessageBoxIcon.Question)
If iexit = DialogResult.Yes Then
Application.Exit()
End If
End Sub

Private Sub BtXoa_17_Click(ByVal sender As System.Object, ByVal e As System.EventArgs) Handles BtXoa_17.Click
Dim ptu As ListViewItem
ptu = Lv_17.SelectedItems(0)
ptu.Remove()
End Sub

Private Sub BtLuu_17_Click(ByVal sender As System.Object, ByVal e As System.EventArgs) Handles BtLuu_17.Click
Dim luu As New IO.StreamWriter(FileNhap)
For Each ptu As ListViewItem In Lv_17.Items
luu.WriteLine(ptu.Text & " || " & ptu.SubItems(1).Text & " || " & ptu.SubItems(2).Text & " || " & ptu.SubItems(3).Text & " || " & ptu.SubItems(4).Text & " || " & ptu.SubItems(5).Text & " || ")
Next
luu.Close()
End Sub
